    "### Praca domowa nr 1 - Reinforcement learning (10-ręki bandyta)\n", 
    "\n", 
    "#### Problem wielorękiego bandyty\n", 
    "Na zajęciach rozważaliśmy zadanie wielorękiego bandyty:\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Mamy wiele maszyn, z których każde ma pewną nieznaną funkcję nagrody. \"Granie\" polega na wyborze maszyny, od której nagrodę otrzymamy. Celem jest granie tak, aby zdobyć sumarycznie jak największą nagrodę.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "#### Eksploracja kontra eksploatacja\n", 
    "Aby zdobyć dużą nagrodę, agent chciałby grać często na maszynie, która do tej pory się sprawdzała. Powinien jednak czasem grać na tych mniej obiecujących, bo być może okażą się one lepsze.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "#### Zadanie\n", 
    "Zreprodukuj obrazek 2.3 ze strony 34 \"Reinforcement Learning: An Introduction\" Sutton, Barto. Czyli:\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Estymuj wartość średnią bandyty przy pomocy wzoru Q_{n+1} = Q_n + alpha_n* (R_n - Q_n), gdzie alpha = 0.1.\n", 
    "Porównaj 2 podejścia:\n", 
    "1. eps-greedy epsilon = 0.1 , gdzie Q_1=0.\n", 
    "2. greedy gdzie Q_1=5.\n", 
    "Narysuj wykres 2D, gdzie na osi OX będzie liczba gier, a na osi OY % wyborów najlepszego bandyty.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Mamy 10 bandytów:\n", 
    "1. N(0.1,1)\n", 
    "2-10. N(0,1)" 
   ],

    "import numpy as np\n", 
    "from itertools import accumulate\n", 
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n", 
    "import seaborn as sns\n", 
    "import random"

    "#Generating rewards for the bandits, determining the parameters\n", 
    "def RewardDrawing(i):\n", 
    "    if i==0:\n", 
    "        return np.random.normal(0.1, 1)\n", 
    "    else:\n", 
    "        return np.random.normal(0,1)\n", 
    "    \n", 
    "iter=10000 #nr of iterations, there are 1000 in the book, but I wanted to see how it looks for more iterations\n", 
    "N_greedy = [0 for _ in range(10)] #nr of selections for each of the bandits by the greedy agent\n", 
    "N_eps_greedy = [0 for _ in range(10)] #Number of selections for each of the bandits by the eps_greedy agent\n", 
    "Q_eps_greedy = [0 for _ in range(10)] \n", 
    "Q_greedy = [5 for _ in range(10)]\n", 
    "epsilon=0.1\n", 
    "alpha=0.1\n", 
    "optimal_bandit=0 #highest expected reward\n", 
    "optimal_percentage_eps_greedy=[0 for _ in range(iter)] #(nr of the best bandit selections)/(nr of all selections)*100% by the eps_greedy agent\n", 
    "optimal_percentage_greedy=[0 for _ in range(iter)] #(nr of the best bandit selections)/(nr of all selections)*100% by the greedy agent" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "collapsed": false, 
    "ExecuteTime": { 
     "end_time": "2024-03-28T21:27:57.594503Z", 
     "start_time": "2024-03-28T21:27:57.569761Z" 
    }

   "source": [ 
    "#eps_greedy\n", 
    "for i in range(iter):\n", 
    "    if random.random() < epsilon:\n", 
    "        bandit = random.randint(0,9)\n", 
    "    else:\n", 
    "        bandit =  random.choice([i for i, x in enumerate(Q_eps_greedy) if x == max(Q_eps_greedy)])\n", 
    "        \n", 
    "    reward = RewardDrawing(bandit)\n", 
    "    N_eps_greedy[bandit] += 1\n", 
    "    Q_eps_greedy[bandit] += (reward-Q_eps_greedy[bandit])*alpha\n", 
    "    optimal_percentage_eps_greedy[i] = N_eps_greedy[optimal_bandit]/(i+1)*100\n", 
    "#greedy\n", 
    "for j in range(iter):\n", 
    "    bandit = random.choice([i for i, x in enumerate(Q_greedy) if x == max(Q_greedy)])\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    reward = RewardDrawing(bandit)\n", 
    "    N_greedy[bandit] += 1\n", 
    "    Q_greedy[bandit] += (reward-Q_greedy[bandit])*alpha\n", 
    "    optimal_percentage_greedy[j] = N_greedy[optimal_bandit]/(j+1)*100" 
   ],
